\"github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.31.2\", \"path\": \"source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.cc\", \"symbol\": \"PrometheusStatsFormatter::statsAsPrometheus\"}\n  ],\n  \"text\": \"The Envoy stats system is implemented in envoyproxy/envoy across multiple layers: (1) Core API interfaces in envoy/stats/ define the Stats::Scope hierarchy, Stats::Store, Stats::Sink, and Stats::Allocator interfaces. (2) The Stats::Scope hierarchy is implemented by two main classes: ThreadLocalStoreImpl::ScopeImpl (source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h) which is thread-local and provides hierarchical scope management with proper reference counting, and IsolatedScopeImpl (source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h) used in tests. (3) The SymbolTable (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h) manages efficient string interning of metric names using a two-level encoding scheme to reduce memory usage. StatNamePool (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h) provides pre-allocated storage for symbolized stat names, enabling fast allocation and deallocation. (4) Tag extraction from metric names is implemented through the TagExtractor hierarchy in source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h and tag_extractor_impl.cc. Multiple implementations exist: TagExtractorStdRegexImpl (using std::regex), TagExtractorRe2Impl (using RE2), TagExtractorTokensImpl (for token-based extraction), and TagExtractorFixedImpl (for fixed tag values). These classes extract tags by matching regular expressions against stat names and building remove_characters intervals. (5) The TagProducerImpl (source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h and tag_producer_impl.cc) coordinates tag extraction, managing a collection of TagExtractors organized with prefix-based optimization in tag_extractor_prefix_map_. Default extractors are defined in source/common/config/well_known_names.cc. (6) Stat sinks dispatch metrics to various backends: Statsd sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/) implements both UDP and TCP variants through statsd.h/cc with configurable prefix and tag format support. Dog StatsD sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/) is DogStatsD-compatible. Graphite StatsD sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/) emits Graphite-compatible tags. Prometheus output is implemented through PrometheusStatsFormatter (source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.h and prometheus_stats.cc) which sanitizes metric names, formats tags, and renders counters, gauges, histograms, and text readouts in Prometheus exposition format. Metrics service sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/) dispatches to gRPC services using MetricsServiceSink template. OpenTelemetry sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/) converts metrics to OTLP format with tag extraction. Hystrix sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/) formats histogram data for Hystrix command metrics. Wasm sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/) enables custom stat processing via WASM modules. (7) Core store implementations: ThreadLocalStoreImpl (source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h and thread_local_store.cc) is the production thread-local store managing per-thread caches, scopes, and metric allocation. AllocatorImpl (source/common/stats/allocator_impl.h and allocator_impl.cc) handles counter, gauge, and histogram allocation with symbol table integration. IsolatedStoreImpl (source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h and isolated_store_impl.cc) is used for testing with a single-threaded implementation. (8) The allocation pipeline uses MetricImpl template (source/common/stats/metric_impl.h and metric_impl.cc) for counters and gauges, HistogramImpl (source/common/stats/histogram_impl.h and histogram_impl.cc) for histograms, and deferred creation patterns (source/common/stats/deferred_creation.h) to lazy-allocate metrics on first access. is implemented in envoyproxy/envoy across multiple layers: (1) Core API interfaces in envoy/stats/ define the Stats::Scope hierarchy, Stats::Store, Stats::Sink, and Stats::Allocator interfaces. (2) The Stats::Scope hierarchy is implemented by two main classes: ThreadLocalStoreImpl::ScopeImpl (source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h) which is thread-local and provides hierarchical scope management with proper reference counting, and IsolatedScopeImpl (source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h) used in tests. (3) The SymbolTable (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h) manages efficient string interning of metric names using a two-level encoding scheme to reduce memory usage. StatNamePool (source/common/stats/symbol_table.h) provides pre-allocated storage for symbolized stat names, enabling fast allocation and deallocation. (4) Tag extraction from metric names is implemented through the TagExtractor hierarchy in source/common/stats/tag_extractor_impl.h and tag_extractor_impl.cc. Multiple implementations exist: TagExtractorStdRegexImpl (using std::regex), TagExtractorRe2Impl (using RE2), TagExtractorTokensImpl (for token-based extraction), and TagExtractorFixedImpl (for fixed tag values). These classes extract tags by matching regular expressions against stat names and building remove_characters intervals. (5) The TagProducerImpl (source/common/stats/tag_producer_impl.h and tag_producer_impl.cc) coordinates tag extraction, managing a collection of TagExtractors organized with prefix-based optimization in tag_extractor_prefix_map_. Default extractors are defined in source/common/config/well_known_names.cc. (6) Stat sinks dispatch metrics to various backends: Statsd sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/statsd/) implements both UDP and TCP variants through statsd.h/cc with configurable prefix and tag format support. Dog StatsD sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/dog_statsd/) is DogStatsD-compatible. Graphite StatsD sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/graphite_statsd/) emits Graphite-compatible tags. Prometheus output is implemented through PrometheusStatsFormatter (source/server/admin/prometheus_stats.h and prometheus_stats.cc) which sanitizes metric names, formats tags, and renders counters, gauges, histograms, and text readouts in Prometheus exposition format. Metrics service sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/metrics_service/) dispatches to gRPC services using MetricsServiceSink template. OpenTelemetry sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/open_telemetry/) converts metrics to OTLP format with tag extraction. Hystrix sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/hystrix/) formats histogram data for Hystrix command metrics. Wasm sink (source/extensions/stat_sinks/wasm/) enables custom stat processing via WASM modules. (7) Core store implementations: ThreadLocalStoreImpl (source/common/stats/thread_local_store.h and thread_local_store.cc) is the production thread-local store managing per-thread caches, scopes, and metric allocation. AllocatorImpl (source/common/stats/allocator_impl.h and allocator_impl.cc) handles counter, gauge, and histogram allocation with symbol table integration. IsolatedStoreImpl (source/common/stats/isolated_store_impl.h and isolated_store_impl.cc) is used for testing with a single-threaded implementation. (8) The allocation pipeline uses MetricImpl template (source/common/stats/metric_impl.h and metric_impl.cc) for counters and gauges, HistogramImpl (source/common/stats/histogram_impl.h and histogram_impl.cc) for histograms, and deferred creation patterns (source/common/stats/deferred_creation.h) to lazy-allocate metrics on first access. (9) Additional components: StatsMatcher (source/common/stats/stats_matcher_impl.h) filters which stats are created based on configuration; StatMerger (source/common/stats/stat_merger.cc) combines stats from multiple sources using both symbolic and dynamic pools; TagUtility (source/common/stats/tag_utility.cc) provides utilities for tag manipulation and StatName operations. The system achieves lock-free access on the fast path through thread-local caching while maintaining consistent symbol tables and tag extraction across the cluster, enabling efficient metric collection and dispatch to multiple backends with tags properly extracted for Prometheus and other tagged-metric systems.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
